南京支社
一、概況
南京支社書記 季傷凡

爲社所爲一個時期．＇第二是從五台山村十

九號搬到九號，再搬到一號為一個時期·,

第三是從新社所建築起到落成爲一
o

南京支社這個名稱幷不是很舊的，上禕支
社，北平支社，天津支社等都是牠的老大

或在分開說一說

第一時期在國府建都南京之前，本社一

··4

哥。蓮位小兄弟年缸雖靑，但是長得很肥 同仁在南京者為數極少，邛涵祇有位 三 ，除了上海支社外，要稱牠最胖 了 現在 1
1 有社員六十人 I 眞是後來居上

°到了國府逵都南京，一般官迷知潮湧來

，我們仁社同仁當然不能例外，所以人就
.

南京支社的歷史，可以分做三個階級，第 忽然多起來了；但是那個時俟，大皆總以
·

一是自國府建都南京租定五台山村十九號 為南京儆首都是靠不隹的，總以為國民政

__

-

8

府基礎沒有稔固，所以一般官迷果然來得 後來又從九號搬到一號，沒有說難五台山

很多，但是小胆的官迷，仍舊是裹足不前 唄範圍，但總覺搬一次好一次。有了社所
-

'H匾到程定五台山村十九號為社所，自 ，我們就等干有了一個家，同仁時常可以

七＾人增加到十餘人，而二十人，而二 十 到 那面打牌色桂洧暹及敍談，平常開會，

亦就有了着落，社員間的成情，不知不覺 餘人。在沒有程定社所取前，南京同仁每

為 同仁寄宿之用，程經遺，黃金濤，何 洒棨館，有時在作東的公館裏，那個時 侯 5 培

1.

＿一一

，陳紹由同仁的公辉是同仁常常去的。 元等許多同仁都隹過，對于沒有家眷的同

第二時期 國民政府的基礎漸漸兒受一般 仁，子以十分的便利。在這個時期內，社

H , 員自二十餘人增加到 ＝ 人，而三十餘人 人信仰了，南京為首都又慢慢兒覺得不生

0 像這樣人口增加的速度， 問題了，小胆的官迷，亦偷偷撲摸的來了 ，而四十餘人

，本社同仁因此一天多似一天，原程五台世界上任何地力沒有的1 罷 第三時期 山村十九號社所覺得太小，就搬到九號，

人的慾荃是沒有滿足的，越

l

l

的比從前親密了。社所樓上有臥室三間， 月見面一次，士同仁輪流作束，有時借用

.r

9

初沒有社所，就想租賃一個社所，猩貨了 我們的新社所樓上全為臥房，共五間，另

幾時，拖覺得不痛快，而且社員增加到有 四術生設備，樓下為兩大間，兩小間，兩

十人了，區磊社所實不鈞應用，所以有 大間一為客廳，一君鈸麾，中間隔以絲絨

人創議自己來造一個社所，主張景力者為 鐮子，氣派很大，客痣內陳設，亦核大方
't是 ll 陳逸凡，姚克家等同仁 一部份同仁
·-－－－一一

，客廳鈸藹面積亦不小，婆起來可以放十

誓酒席，元＾日開耆那天，除了上 以為茲事體大，須審塡考慮，還有一部份

－一

同仁恐怡「後雖為濟」，所以先舉出了 了三位老大哥外，其餘各地支社及社6 員買

個委員會，孝慮了好幾個月，才決定動手電，像雪片飛求。那天晚上，由虞國國
0

人藺幕，儀式概简關而有意義。閉幕後， 其間知何籌款，知有打樣，知何督造等

等問題，全中委員會負責辦理。本社自造 由 1111 同仁等楞繼濱說，後來就
A 日開幕 社所遂千本年一月底完成，二月
0

聚餐，到有租員及眷屬一百二十餘人，分
對干這個新社所最勞苦功高者，是姚克 家同仁，我們不能不威激他的。

十一棹坐，其熱蘭情疣，實有非筆墨所能

形容。餐畢全體照桂，最後還有中西音樂

10

助興＇至午夜焓各盡歡而散。

聚餐主人由同仁輪流，每次四位，菜是自

自新社所落成以後，大皆更覺得好像自己 己廚房微的o 每次座談會，講一個題目，

由一位同仁主講，講畢再互旌討論趼究， 的家了，可以隨時來社敍談，宴客，消遣

彼此得益不淺。 。現在地方寛敞，所以每次開會，一點不
覺得像從前那樣的揸了。

對干這一次本支社社所落成開萘，各地支

社所幷備有網球步一個，完全虞社 圉及 圜同仁電賀及增送各種禮物，我們
瑳到這種的消息。

1 機會，再向大皆表示威謝，我們幷且 借 捐賚建築，有網球癌的同仁，當然很高個 興

l ＿ ．這個機會，敬祝全體同仁康縫，J 有l 是 會

1 亦就是大家的 京 ，請弗忘記到我們的 現在社員人數，已經到了六十之數，南 七 ＾

史，而其迤展成箝較着，引越國人深切之

I

錄

,,

民圉二十一年至現在

注意者，更為最近四五年事，本人以爲中 潭一段軍用路，為程一百苹里，此為我國
國公路建設，可分後列三時期：

--

民國二年湖南都督倡議築造長沙至湘

(－)草藺築路時期
民國元年至十六年

省道辦事處，此為各省設立公路主管機關

`先 7河 ] 。民國七年北京政府倡辦張家口至

－一

庫倫長途汽車路駛行長途汽車，凡此皆公

路建設第一時期中主要各事，可得而述者

西北考察後原想

荘澤宣同仁在杭州支瓩座談會嶠稿

西北的墩育並不茹我們理惹的落後。 食。他們隹的是土房房內有一大坑，十餘

西北學生的刻苦，確為東南所不及。西北 人不分關冬天坑下蟯馬糞穿的衣服，一律

布 衣學生赤工人的分別很微，連虔鞋都沒 的學生，有許卒，在閉學時負來幾捏薨粉 製

有，只穿布鞋。在訓育方面，亦為東南所 成餅食，吃的時侯，今年開水一泡肉類吃不

不及。在西北，學生老遠就向先生很恭敬 郅，菜蔬亦有時吃不到。西北的人吃兩餐

的行禮，諸茹此類的事情很多，學風很好 害中一餐沒有，平均每人花二元一月的伙

207

And H. C. Tsao （ 趙運文） on the same page of "missing brothers'', this brother can be found on page 35 as a member of Shanghai Chapter under the name （趙鴻酞 Bro. Tsao is in a serious condition of health. Just after last year's P. L . Conference I called at his home to convey to him the best wishes of the fraternity . Although he could understand what I said, he was unable to express himself as he had lost the power of speech. He has been bed-ridden for nearly two years (I see a reference to him on page 8 of the last issue of the P. L. Report)

P. U. M. C. Hospital, Peiping. July 26, 1936. Dear Bro. Wong: I wish to thank you for your nice letter inquiring about my condition-I am glad to say that I have continued to improve and hope that I may not have to stay in the hospital as long as others. I also wish to add my congratulation to your E'xcellent showing of the Fratern· ity publication. I only received them yesterday but I am impressed about the excellent material it contained. In every way it was a greatly impro~ed publication. I am sure
9S

every one will feel proud of your eifort. I am enclosing my vote for these two candidates as I said I only got them yesterday so I am sending you today . Better late than never.

I hope it may be of some use. Kindly convey to the officers of the Fraternity my thanks for the remem· brances they have for me and the letter ns publisher!. I am sure the work in Nanking will prosper, and I hope to see you all when I have occasion to come down south next time. With best regards. Fraterna11y yours, Sam Zia.
LS

P .S. Kindly excuse my writing in pencil as I am writing it in bed..

A WORD FROM THE EUROPEAN CHAPTER
oo

Dear B r o t h e r s : . . . . , On behalf of the European Chapter, I wish to congratulate you as the New Manager of the U.S. Chapter, and send you all our best-wishes. We are very proud

I

of the U.S. Chapter, being so well conducted and full of everlasting sporot of all those who are attached to it.

It is decidedly

true that co-operation of every one in the

organisation is an essential element towards success. The European Chapter is getting on fine, but it is a great pity that we are all

scattered in different places, with the result that we have not had much meeting.

opportunity of

Recently, three Brothers, left for China, Brother N. L. Lieu, Brother Li,

Brother Lieu and Brother Wu are believed to come to the United States for a short stay. I hope they w,ill meet you all somewhere. Regarding your suggestion to present a gift to our new Headquarters in Would it not be a good idea
~

Nanking, we are just thinking of doing the same thing.

if both the U. S. Chapter and the E~ropean Cha(:>ter join together to make such la · presentation? We think we can afford to contribute about 4 pounds. ($20, gold), so if

you will also contribute that amount, it will mean about $130.- in Chinese currency. We send a dollar draft to Nanking, requesting them to purchase any article they need, and inscribe it with the words "From Brothers of United States and European Chapters".

If you should think •the amount is to small, please let us know and we will consider it
agam.
I6C

Z6£

If you think our suggestion is good, please remit to us 4 pounds, or we will
send to yon the equivalent of 4 pounds, in order to remit to Nanking in a lump sum.

I am enclosing herewith a list of members of the E.uropean Chapter, which
please publish in your next circulation. With kindest regards to you all, Yours fraternally,

T. Y. Lee

P. N. M. C. Hospital Peiping, Nov. 4, 1936. Dear Bro. Wang, Your telegram congratulating me on my convalescence was duly received. e~tremely grateful to the thoughtfulness the officers of the Fraternity have given me. I am I am
~

orry I did not find it possible to acknowledge the previous letters and gifts of flowers earlier but I am deeply touched just the same. Certainly your actions have proven the kindly spirit of the officers toward every brother and I hope every one will be able to eopy the action of our leaders. Kindly express to these officers, not excluding yourself, my gratitude and best regard.
J am sorry to say that as yet, althongh I am much improved, I am not able to

l

1eave the hospital. However, I trust that it shall not be long now before I shall be able to nsume my activities. At the same time I must express my regret in not being able to send
IZV

zz<

you the data you need for the directory as 1 have not at hand a recent photo for that purpose. I shall, however, try to send you as soon as I find it possible to do so. May I congratulate you on the arrival of the baby? I trust both the mother and the child are doing well. With best regards, Fruternally yours, Sam Zia.
